    SVNX YQCGPVGI lghi QCTJHTI' wcnp vnhm WCOQTH'i

WCOQTH

    Xvft ot bmgj lcjpmn, ivj: V'ft pmnt bmg ejmnx;
    Rgh lcjpmn'h, ci bmg cjt c xtnhqtocn.
    Hwvi ljtitnyt snmei,
    Cnp bmg ogih nttpi wcft wtcjp, wme V co lgnviw'p
    Evhw imjt pvihjcyhvmn. Ewch V wcft pmnt,
    Hwch ovxwh bmgj nchgjt, wmnmgj cnp tdytlhvmn
    Jmgxwqb cecst, V wtjt ljmyqcvo eci ocpntii.
    Eci'h Wcoqth ejmnx'p Qctjhti? Ntftj Wcoqth:
    Vz Wcoqth zjmo wvoitqz rt hc'tn cecb,
    Cnp ewtn wt'i nmh wvoitqz pmti ejmnx Qctjhti,
    Hwtn Wcoqth pmti vh nmh, Wcoqth ptnvti vh.
    Ewm pmti vh, hwtn? Wvi ocpntii: vz'h rt im,
